714 <h1>

715Best CBD Oil for Pain: Top 5 Brands in 2021 &#038; Buyer’s Guide</h1>

716

717 <span class="metadata">

718<a href="https://ministryofhemp.com/blog/author/moh/" title="Posts by Ministry of Hemp" rel="author">

719Ministry of Hemp</a>

720 / April 23, 2021 / <a href="#comments">

721No Comments</a>

722</span>

723

724 </div>

725

726 </div>

727

728

729 <div class="row">

730

731 <div class="col col-xsmall--12">

732

733 <p>

734Due to the incredible healing properties of some of cannabis plants’ chemical compounds, people have for centuries sought them out. But it was recently when one of its key compounds – a cannabinoid to be exact – drew the attention of both scientists and the common man.&nbsp;</p>

735

736

737

738

739<p>

740And that is CBD. This chemical compound is available in many forms like CBD Oil, <a data-lasso-id="9517" href="https://ministryofhemp.com/blog/best-cbd-gummies/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">

741Gummies</a>

742, <a data-lasso-id="9518" href="https://ministryofhemp.com/blog/best-cbd-topicals-cream/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">

743Creams</a>

744 in the market today. However, the most popular form is <a href="https://ministryofhemp.com/blog/best-cbd-tinctures/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10310">

745CBD oil</a>

746, especially when it comes to combating painful and inflammatory conditions. </p>

747

748

749

750

751<p>

752It has been used for a ton of health conditions, including arthritis, chronic pain, osteoarthritis, and common inflammation of various parts of the body, including joints.&nbsp;</p>

753

754

755

756

757<p>

758Cannabidiol or CBD, as we commonly call it, is also reported to provide other health benefits, including better sleep, reduced anxiety, and improved immunity.</p>

759

760

761

762

763<p>

764But not all CBD oil available in the market are good or genuine. Due to the growing demand for this compound, many wellness companies have entered the CBD industry. This abundance of options not only overwhelms a user but has also opened up the scope for many fake companies to abuse the trust of unwary customers.</p>

765

766

767

768

769<p>

770That is why we continually keep you updated on the best and most effective, high-quality CBD products available in the market, which are safe, potent, and reasonably priced – so that you don’t get fooled by shrewd vendors trying to push useless or harmful products in the garb of “Authentic” or “Natural” CBD products.&nbsp;</p>

771

772

773

774

775<p>

776To select the best CBD oil for pain, we took several critical steps to ensure you get the best of everything. Here they are:&nbsp;</p>

777

778

779

780

781<ul>

782<li>

783We sought the opinion of some of the industry’s renowned experts, including researchers, testers, and long-time consumers. Their experience and understanding helped us select from around 50 brands of CBD oil brands in the market.</li>

784<li>

785We also studied over 5,000 user reviews, including those on company websites, social media platforms, blogs, and open forums, to get a sense of how these brands have fared in the market.</li>

786<li>

787We reached out to our readers through a survey, in which over 8,000 of our email subscribers gave their take on these different brands of CBD oil.</li>

788<li>

789We took a closer look at each of their brand websites to check the veracity of some of the critical information needed to understand the brands and their products. These aspects included transparency, reliability, and sense of responsibility of the brands, the technology utilized by the brands, their farming, extraction, and manufacturing practices, etc. We also looked at their certificates of analysis (sent by third-party labs) to check their ingredients, safety profile, and cannabinoid content.&nbsp;</li>

790<li>

791Finally, we tested over 15 brands of the most recommended CBD oil brands to verify the authenticity of all their claims as well as to compare their quality and efficacy against their prices. We wanted to make sure that we only recommend brands that give you value for money.</li>

792</ul>

793

794

795

796

2763<h3 id="h-selecting-the-cbd-oil-brands-for-pain-critical-factors">

2764<strong>

2765Selecting The CBD Oil Brands for Pain: Critical Factors</strong>

2766</h3>

2767

2768

2769

2770

2771<ul>

2772<li>

2773<strong>

2774Hemp Source: </strong>

2775<a href="https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/31447137/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10311">

2776CBD oil</a>

2777 comes from hemp plants, as they have low tetrahydrocannabinol content (THC; the psychoactive component of cannabis plants, high levels of which are present in marijuana). Where and how hemp is cultivated determines the quality of the extract. Hemp plants, grown in the US (and parts of the EU), are safer and more potent, as they are grown under strict guidelines, bound by federal regulations. They are generally organically grown, contain very little THC (&lt;0.3%), and contain no harmful chemicals, GMO, or heavy metals. The US Hemp Authority is the regulatory body for all extracts derived from US-grown industrial/agricultural hemp.</li>

2778<li>

2779<strong>

2780Extract Types:</strong>

2781 Hemp extracts are generally of three types, i.e., full-spectrum hemp extracts that contain all plant nutrients of cannabis (cannabinoids (including traces of THC), terpenes, flavonoids, fatty acids, minerals, vitamins, and proteins), broad-spectrum extracts that contain all the same components of cannabis plants, except THC, and CBD isolates that contain only pure CBD extract. While the two former types are known to provide the entourage effect, people who need to undergo regular drug tests prefer the isolate CBD extracts. </li>

2782<li>

2783<strong>

2784Potency: </strong>

2785The CBD content is the most important part of assessing a CBD product’s standard. Usually designated in milligrams (mg), this is what directly determines the tincture’s efficacy. The more concentrated the oil, the more effective it is. That does not, however, mean that you take more CBD than you need. This is to help you determine your dosage. Reputed brands clearly mention their CBD content in their label. So, you can dose yourself properly. Admittedly, a person needs higher doses of CBD for pain compared to mental issues like anxiety and depression. However, taking too much does you no good. This is why the brands offer variations in CBD concentration. The effect of CBD does not depend on potency alone. A 25mg full-spectrum CBD oil could be more effective than a 100mg CBD isolate. So, it is best to start with a low dose. </li>

2786<li>

2787<strong>

2788Container Size Variants: </strong>

2789This is another way that brands help you dose better, i.e., by giving you variations in container sizes. Brands often provide variations like 15ml, 30ml, and 60ml in CBD oil with varying CBD concentrations. This means you can consume it at different times at different dosages as per requirement. </li>

2790<li>

2791<strong>

2792Ingredients: </strong>

2793Besides CBD, the other ingredients also play an important role in the product’s ultimate effect. Check out the ingredients and their quantities to know more about the product’s formulation, the combination of ingredients, and the overall quality. Ingredients like carrier oil, flavorings, and add-ons are meant to enhance CBD’s effects and help its easy absorption. Besides, reputed brands ensure to exclude all contaminants, synthetic chemicals, and high levels of THC from their hemp extracts. Always choose CBD oil made from naturally sourced ingredients, better still, from organically grown ones and those that are devoid of potential allergens.</li>

2794<li>

2795<strong>

2796Taste/Flavor:</strong>

2797 Although it may seem like a non-issue, aroma or flavor play a significant role in managing the overall experience, especially when someone is in extreme pain. Stimulation of our senses can help alleviate or exacerbate the condition. The more pleasant the taste, the better will be the user&#8217;s experience. While strong flavors could give you a headache, a bitter hempy flavor may dampen the experience. That’s why brands offer a range of delicious flavors to choose from. Additionally, natural and organic flavorings ensure a safer and better effect on the body.</li>

2798<li>

2799<strong>

2800Third-party lab test: </strong>

2801A reputable, transparent company will take the responsibility towards their customers seriously. They would subject their products to third-party lab testing to confirm the products’ safety, efficacy, and due presence of necessary ingredients. In other words, independent laboratories can testify in an unbiased manner to the quality, safety, and content claims made by a CBD brand with scientific evidence. Do not buy from a CBD brand that hasn’t been reviewed by an independent lab.</li>

2802<li>

2803<strong>

2804Brand Reputation:</strong>

2805 Because the CBD industry is relatively new and the Food and Drug Administration doesn’t regulate all CBD products, a customer needs to consider the reputation of a company before purchasing their products. This is how you can find out whether the CBD oil brand values their customers and their feedback on what they sell.</li>

2806<li>

2807<strong>

2808Transparency: </strong>

2809Companies that are keen on revealing their business practices publicly are open to discussions and customer opinions. Information on the farming practices, manufacturing, extraction, their technology, and the testing processes, along with independent lab results instill a sense of reliability among consumers.</li>

2810<li>

2811<strong>

2812Customer Service:</strong>

2813 Customer support is critical to ensuring happy customers. This maintains the brand’s reputation. Since this is the first and last line of engagement with the customers, a brand makes sure that it is at least as good as the products themselves, if not better.</li>

2814<li>

2815<strong>

2816Company Policies: </strong>

2817The shipping, return, and refund policies must be customer-centric, especially in a competitive market like the CBD industry. Given the high prices of CBD products, free shipping, confirmed delivery, easy returns, and money-back guarantees are important to stay on in the business. </li>

2818<li>

2819<strong>

2820Online Shopping Experience:</strong>

2821 A brand website must be easy to navigate, should provide ample information on the benefits of their products, offer easy shopping and checkout experience to make the overall shopping experience better.</li>

2822</ul>

2823

2835

2836

2837

2838

2839<p>

2840There are several methods that can be used to manufacture CBD products. But not all are made equal. Some are perfectly safe, and others may be risky due to the use of toxic solvents.</p>

2883

2884

2885<p>

2886The most reputable companies tend to use CO2 supercritical/subcritical extraction because it is one of the best ways to get a high yield of CBD without any exposure to toxic chemicals. It’s really the gold standard as far as CBD extraction goes.</p>

2887

2888

2889

2890

2891<p>

2892When looking for a CBD oil product for your <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC2503660/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10312">

2893pain relief</a>

2894, ensure that the brand is transparent about its production process. If there’s little to no information is available, this is usually a huge red flag.</p>

2895

2898

2899<h3>

2900Third-party tested</h3>

2901

2902

2903

2904

2905<p>

2906Top tier CBD oil brands will usually boast that their products have been third-party lab tested. It’s a great selling point and helps to bring validity and transparency to the brand.</p>

2907

2908

2909

2910

2911<p>

2912For the consumer, it also provides some reassurance that what is claimed on the label is accurate, and that the item is safe for consumption. So, before you purchase that CBD tincture to relieve your pain and other symptoms, make sure that the item has been third-party verified. The actual results of the test should be available for customers to review. When you’re examining this information, ensure that it’s up to date and that the tests have been conducted within the last 6 months.</p>

2963<h3>

2964Ingredients on the label</h3>

2965

2966

2967

2968

2969<p>

2970Transparent product labelling is absolutely essential for any consumable good. After all, you need to know exactly what you’re putting into your body.</p>

2971

2972

2973

2974

2975<p>

2976There’s no way to tell if a CBD product is the best suited for your pain solely based on the nice graphics on the label. But the list of ingredients and nutrition facts on the back will certainly go a long way. The two main components that are usually included in a tincture are CBD and a carrier oil like MCT (often based on coconut oil) or hemp seed oil. Apart from that, you may observe fractional percentages of other cannabinoids on the lab test results.</p>

2977

2978

2979

2980

2981<p>

2982Some brands may also offer their own special blend of herbs in addition to CBD, to enhance pain relief. Reputable companies usually give a detailed breakdown of all the ingredients included, and their respective percentages. If this information is obscure or non-existent, then we recommend you proceed with caution.</p>

2983

2984

2985

2986

2987<h3>

2988Reviews and recommendations</h3>

2989

2990

2991

2992

2993<p>

2994The internet makes it possible for us to get an idea of how a product will work before we make any monetary investment. Reviews and recommendations go a long way when shopping for CBD oil. Every brand will claim to provide the best CBD products for pain and the world of symptoms.</p>

2995

2996

2997

2998

2999<p>

3000So, it helps to look beyond the marketing pitch and listen to the opinions of actual consumers or trustworthy sources. Always look for reviews and recommendations online before making a purchase. If the reviews are good then it will most likely be a good product, and if they’re bad, then you just saved yourself a bad experience.</p>

3002

3003

3004

3005<p>

3006In addition to sites like Ministry of Hemp, we often recommend the <a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/cbd" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10313">

3007CBD subreddit on Reddit</a>

3008 as a great resource for connecting with other CBD consumers.</p>

3012

3013<h2 id="h-types-of-pain-related-issues-that-cbd-can-combat">

3014<strong>

3015Types of Pain Related Issues That CBD Can Combat</strong>

3016</h2>

3017

3018

3019

3020

3021<p>

3022Based on medical research, CBD can help get relief from pain, associated with different kinds of medical conditions. Some of them are elaborated here:&nbsp;</p>

3023

3024

3025

3026

3027<h3 id="h-arthritis">

3028<strong>

3029Arthritis&nbsp;</strong>

3030</h3>

3031

3032

3033

3034

3035<p>

3036<a href="http://blog.arthritis.org/news/patients-tell-us-cbd-use/" data-lasso-id="9526">

3037Arthritis Foundation</a>

3038’s recent survey found that 29% of their respondents used CBD, most of whom seemed to have benefited from its use. While scientists are still studying the veracity of CBD’s efficacy in combating arthritic pain, some studies have found promising results. In animal studies, nevertheless, CBD has been found to possess anti-inflammatory and pain-relieving properties, without posing any threat or side effects.&nbsp;</p>

3039

3040

3041

3042

3043<h3 id="h-chronic-pain">

3044<strong>

3045Chronic Pain</strong>

3046</h3>

3047

3048

3049

3050

3051<p id="h-unfortunately-chronic-pain-affects-a-large-majority-of-people-all-over-the-world-at-some-point-in-their-lives-although-opioids-are-usually-used-to-relieve-pain-they-have-many-adverse-effects-and-even-tend-to-cause-dependence-and-addiction-cbd-is-proposed-as-a-better-and-safer-alternative-to-opioids-for-pain-relief">

3052Unfortunately, <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC7204604/" data-lasso-id="9527">

3053chronic pain</a>

3054 affects a large majority of people all over the world at some point in their lives. Although opioids are usually used to relieve pain, they have many adverse effects and even tend to cause dependence and addiction. CBD is proposed as a better and safer alternative to opioids for pain relief.</p>

3055

3056

3057

3058

3059<h3 id="h-migraine">

3060<strong>

3061Migraine</strong>

3062</h3>

3063

3064

3065

3066

3067<p id="h-a-painful-condition-migraine-is-usually-caused-by-stress-anxiety-and-other-chemical-imbalances-within-the-body-tests-using-a-combination-of-cbd-and-thc-have-shown-that-people-can-get-relief-from-migraines-and-improve-their-body-s-overall-capacity-to-manage-pain-in-subjects-in-such-a-test-was-seen-to-experience-relief-from-acute-pain-by-as-much-as-55-additionally-the-frequency-of-migraine-attacks-was-also-reduced-by-40">

3068A painful condition, <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC5928495/" data-lasso-id="9528">

3069migraine</a>

3070 is usually caused by stress, anxiety, and other chemical imbalances within the body. Tests, using a combination of CBD and THC, have shown that people can get relief from migraines and improve their body’s overall capacity to manage pain. In subjects in such a test was seen to experience relief from acute pain by as much as 55%. Additionally, the frequency of migraine attacks was also reduced by 40%.&nbsp;</p>

3071

3072

3073

3074

3075<h3 id="h-cancer-treatment-associated-issues">

3076<strong>

3077Cancer Treatment &amp; Associated Issues</strong>

3078</h3>

3079

3080

3081

3082

3083<p id="h-both-the-effects-and-treatment-of-cancer-are-painful-for-patients-cbd-has-been-found-to-be-effective-in-lowering-both-these-types-of-pain-to-reduce-the-effects-of-cancer-chemotherapy-such-as-pain-vomiting-and-lack-of-appetite-among-patients-the-national-cancer-institute-also-recommends-the-use-of-cbd-it-has-also-been-proven-effective-in-getting-better-pain-relief-than-opioids-without-the-side-effects-associated-with-opioid-use">

3084Both the effects and treatment of cancer are painful for patients. CBD has been found to be effective in lowering both these types of pain.<strong>

3085 </strong>

3086To reduce the effects of cancer chemotherapy, such as pain, vomiting, and lack of appetite among patients, the National Cancer Institute also <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/cam/hp" data-lasso-id="9529">

3087recommends</a>

3088 the use of CBD. It has also been proven effective in getting better pain relief than opioids, without the side effects associated with opioid use.</p>

3093<h3 id="h-multiple-sclerosis-ms">

3094<strong>

3095Multiple Sclerosis (MS)</strong>

3096</h3>

3097

3098

3099

3100

3101<p id="h-ms-is-an-autoimmune-disease-that-affects-a-patient-s-nervous-system-and-thereby-his-her-entire-body-people-with-ms-experience-extremely-painful-muscle-spasms-and-a-lack-of-control-over-their-voluntary-muscles-cbd-oil-use-can-reduce-a-person-s-spasticity-associated-with-ms">

3102MS is an autoimmune disease that affects a patient’s nervous system, and thereby his/her entire body. People with MS experience extremely painful muscle spasms and a lack of control over their voluntary muscles. CBD oil use can <a href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Stuart_Ratcliffe/publication/233770159_A_double-blind_randomized_placebo-controlled_parallel-group_study_of_THCCBD_oromucosal_spray_in_combination_with_the_existing_treatment_regimen_in_the_relief_of_central_neuropathic_pain_in_patients_wi/links/57d8111a08ae6399a39912da/A-double-blind-randomized-placebo-controlled-parallel-group-study-of-THC-CBD-oromucosal-spray-in-combination-with-the-existing-treatment-regimen-in-the-relief-of-central-neuropathic-pain-in-patien.pdf" data-lasso-id="12470">

3103reduce</a>

3104<strong>

3105 </strong>

3106a person’s spasticity associated with MS.&nbsp;</p>

3111<h3 id="h-how-cbd-interacts-with-the-body">

3112<strong>

3113How CBD Interacts With The Body</strong>

3114<strong>

3115?</strong>

3116</h3>

3117

3118

3119

3120

3121<p>

3122All cannabinoids impact the body by interacting with the <a data-lasso-id="9530" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC4789136/">

3123endocannabinoid system</a>

3124. While studies on how it does that are still underway, we do know that cannabinoids like CBD and THC interact by binding directly or indirectly with some of the body’s cannabinoid and non-cannabinoid receptors of the body (quite like the endocannabinoids found within the body). </p>

3125

3126

3127

3128

3129<h3 id="h-research-on-cbd-s-pain-relieving-properties">

3130<strong>

3131Research on CBD&#8217;s Pain-Relieving Properties</strong>

3132</h3>

3133

3134

3135

3136

3137<ul>

3138<li>

3139According to a 2018 <a data-lasso-id="9531" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC6043845/">

3140research</a>

3141 by the <em>

3142National Center for Biotechnology Information</em>

3143, published in the <em>

3144Cannabis and Cannabinoid Research</em>

3145 journal, nearly 62% of the people consuming CBD had a medical condition they were trying to treat. As per the study, among all the different medical conditions, the 3-most common medical conditions CBD is generally used for are to treat pain, <a data-lasso-id="9532" href="https://ministryofhemp.com/blog/best-cbd-oil-for-anxiety/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">

3146anxiety</a>

3147, and depression.</li>

3148<li>

3149As per the <a data-lasso-id="9533" href="https://www.nccih.nih.gov/health/cannabis-marijuana-and-cannabinoids-what-you-need-to-know">

3150National Centers for Complementary and Integrative Health</a>

3151, there is evidence to indicate that cannabis compounds may have modest chronic pain benefits. </li>

3152<li>

3153According to a <a data-lasso-id="9534" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC1575333/">

31542004 study</a>

3155, published in the <em>

3156British Journal of Pharmacology</em>

3157, CBD can relieve pain and inflammation in rat models through TRPV1-receptor-stimulation.</li>

3158<li>

3159A <a data-lasso-id="9535" href="https://journals.lww.com/anesthesia-analgesia/Fulltext/2017/11000/Selective_Cannabinoids_for_Chronic_Neuropathic.32.aspx">

31602017 review</a>

3161 found that CBD helps treat chronic human neuropathy. Researchers examined 11 randomized controlled trials that included 1,219 patients to test the veracity of the claims.</li>

3162<li>

3163According to a <a data-lasso-id="9536" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC7204604/">

31642020 review</a>

3165, CBD may benefit patients with crippling and chronic pain, sleep disturbances, and chronic inflammation. However, the scientists stressed the need for more scientific data to determine CBD’s therapeutic effects and assess its exact efficacy and safe dosage.</li>

3166</ul>

3171<h3>

3172CBD Shows Significant Pain Relief Potential in Scientific Studies</h3>

3173

3174

3175

3176

3177<p>

3178Numerous scientific studies suggest CBD can help with many different forms of pain. In a Feb. 2003 study published in <a href="http://journals.sagepub.com/doi/abs/10.1191/0269215503cr581oa" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10314">

3179Clinical Rehabilitation</a>

3180, a team of researchers from Oxford examined the benefits of CBD, THC, and a combination of both in patients who suffered from &#8220;neurogenic&#8221; pain (meaning their pain originated in their nervous system).</p>

3181

3182

3183

3184

3185<p>

3186Most of the 24 patients in the study suffered from multiple sclerosis, but others had pain from spinal cord injuries or limb amputation. The study&#8217;s subjects regularly took one or more of the substances, or a placebo, at home, for two weeks while periodically reporting into the clinic.</p>

3187

3188

3189

3190

3191<p>

3192&#8220;Pain relief associated <a href="http://ministryofhemp.com/blog/cbd-vs-thc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10315">

3193with both THC and CBD</a>

3194 was significantly superior to placebo,&#8221; the researchers&#8217; wrote. Not only did the patients experience significant relief, but in some cases other unpleasant symptoms like muscle spasms were also alleviated.<br>

3232Current Medical Research and Opinion</a>

3233, also supported the idea that cannabis extracts, including CBD, are especially effective in treating pain caused by multiple sclerosis. The authors looked at six different studies and found they consistently showed &#8220;Cannabinoids &#8230; are effective in treating neuropathic pain in MS.&#8221;</p>

3240&#8220;difficult to manage pain.&#8221;</a>

3241 Rudd&#8217;s report, another &#8220;meta-analysis&#8221; of multiple studies, is especially interesting because he reported that cannabis extracts can offer significant benefits not just when ingested orally, but also when applied topically to the skin. Many consumers have similarly reported receiving relief from <a href="https://ministryofhemp.com/blog/best-cbd-topicals-cream/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10318">

3242topical forms of CBD oil</a>

3243 and psychoactive cannabis.</p>

3248<h3>

3249CBD Oil Offers Relief From Menstrual Cramps to Migraines</h3>

3250

3251

3252

3253

3254<p>

3255To get a wider look at CBD&#8217;s potential benefits, we also searched a variety of anecdotal reports found in blogs and message boards.</p>

3256

3257

3258

3259

3260<p>

3261Pamela Hadfield, a co-founder of the medical cannabis site HelloMD, <a href="https://www.hellomd.com/health-wellness/migraines-how-i-got-off-pain-meds-and-found-relief-with-cannabis" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10319">

3262reported</a>

3263 in July 2015 that she &#8220;started using CBD to manage chronic pain caused by crazy, intense migraines.&#8221; While pharmaceutical drugs left her feeling mentally hazy, CBD seems to offer her immediate relief with few side effects.</p>

3264

3265

3266

3267

3268<p>

3269Similarly, in a <a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/CBD/comments/5ows18/cbd_for_menstrual_cramps_anyone_out_there_using_it/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10320">

3270discussion</a>

3271 last month on Reddit, many Redditors reported CBD quickly eases their menstrual cramps, though the dosage needed varies a great deal from person to person. The Redditors also noticed that the quality of the CBD extract made a big difference in its effectiveness. The source and quality of CBD oil products are vitally important, as we reported last July on Ministry of Hemp, so research all hemp products before you buy them.</p>

3272

3273

3274

3275

3276<p>

3277While many people with chronic pain benefit from CBD oil alone, others receive the most relief from a combination of CBD and THC, which unfortunately remains illegal in many parts of the U.S. For example, Donna Burch, the author of the Fed Up With Fatigue blog, suffers from fibromyalgia, a poorly understood condition that combines debilitating fatigue and insomnia with severe muscle cramps. Burch <a href="http://fedupwithfatigue.com/cbd-oil-and-fibromyalgia/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10321">

3278reported</a>

3279 in Sept. 2015 that while CBD oil seemed to help her pain for a while, it became less effective over time.</p>

3280

3281

3282

3283

3284<p>

3285She ultimately found the most relief from psychoactive cannabis after receiving a permit for legal medical use. In states with medical cannabis programs, many chronic pain patients like <a href="https://www.leafly.com/news/strains-products/what-cannabis-strains-are-high-in-cbd" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-lasso-id="10322">

3286Burch</a>

3287 seek out strains bred to contain high levels of CBD along with THC.</p>

3292<h2 id="h-cbd-dosage-for-pain">

3293<strong>

3294CBD Dosage for Pain</strong>

3295</h2>

3296

3297

3298

3299

3300<p>

3301The effects of CBD may vary from person to person. It largely depends on each person’s unique physiology, metabolism, the severity of the medical condition, form of CBD used, the formulation used by the brand, the purity of the extract used in the formulation, among several other factors.&nbsp;</p>

3302

3303

3304

3305

3306<p>

3307While not all factors can be controlled, like those that are in the hands of the companies making these products, certain things can be controlled by the users.&nbsp;</p>

3308

3309

3310

3311

3312<p>

3313Chronic pain and inflammation could cripple a person and jeopardize his/her normal life. unlike anxiety and depression, pain requires a lot more CBD, i.e., a larger dose.&nbsp;</p>

3314

3315

3316

3317

3318<p>

3319Broadly speaking, some of the patient-centric factors include:</p>

3320

3321

3322

3323

3324<ul>

3325<li>

3326Age</li>

3327<li>

3328Gender</li>

3329<li>

3330Bodyweight</li>

3331<li>

3332Type of pain issues</li>

3333<li>

3334The severity of the patient’s condition</li>

3335<li>

3336The body’s capacity to absorb and metabolize cannabinoids</li>

3337<li>

3338Mode of administration</li>

3339<li>

3340Chemical balance within the patient’s ECS</li>

3341</ul>

3342

3343

3344

3345

3346<p>

3347Usually, a dose of <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC6222489/#sec3-molecules-23-02478title" data-lasso-id="9537">

3348around 2.85 to 50 mg/kg/day</a>

3349&nbsp;is usually therapeutic for and tolerable to humans. Nevertheless, it’s always safer to start with a small dose and gradually titrate the dosage. As soon as you reach the optimal dose, stick to it, without increasing it any further.&nbsp;</p>

3350

3351

3352

3353

3354<p>

3355Lastly, consult a medical practitioner before using CBD for the first time. Since you and your body are new to this substance, it is best to discuss the delivery method and dosage with a certified doctor before going ahead with self-treatment of pain with the help of CBD oil.&nbsp;</p>

3356

3357

3358

3359

3360<h2 id="h-final-thoughts-does-cbd-oil-work-on-pain-issues">

3361<strong>

3362Final Thoughts: Does CBD Oil Work On Pain Issues?</strong>

3363</h2>

3364

3365

3366

3367

3368<p>

3369Although numerous studies have indicated CBD’s efficacy in treating pain, more research is needed, particularly advanced human trials.&nbsp;</p>

3370

3371

3372

3373

3374<p>

3375For now, we can state that the currently available research literature is promising, but not conclusive. Meanwhile, anecdotal evidence has been far more encouraging when it comes to chronic pain treatment.&nbsp;</p>

3376

3377

3378

3379

3380<p>

3381Due to the absence of the intoxicating effects and eventual side effects associated with THC (which is high in marijuana and low in industrial hemp), CBD oil sold by reputed brands have been found to be effective in helping people overcome painful conditions. </p>

3382

3383

3384

3385

3386<p>

3387Our list includes only those brands of products that have proven to be effective against painful health conditions by a large number of people worldwide. So, if you <em>

3388must</em>

3389 use CBD for pain treatment, you can trust these brands to do right by you – in both helping you overcome pain and getting the most out of the money you shell out!</p>
